Selected Speeches of Sun Myung Moon

Compiled by the Sun Myung Moon Speeches Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the Family Federation for World Peace and Unification  Hwang Sun Jo
Rev. Sun Myung Moon, who received the calling for the salvation of humanity from Heaven at the age of 16, has lived his entire life centered on the Heavenly Way with a single-minded focus! Rev. Moon described his life as follows:
"If Reverend Moon has any wealth, it is nothing but the suffering endured for the public good rather than for personal hardship. In social life, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. From the perspective of providence, I tried to suffer more than anyone else. ... Until now, the teacher has received countless opposition and persecution from the nation and the world. I was opposed in America, by Christianity, Judaism, and even communists. Never in history has the world united to attack and eliminate one person like this. In that sense, the teacher is a global champion. However, despite being cursed, I have not been crushed or destroyed. I have come out stronger without the slightest movement. ... Reverend Moon advocates for the liberation of humanity, the liberation of the spirit world, the liberation of hell, and even the liberation of God." (Refer to the Selected Speeches, Volume 105, pages 101-103)
Rev. Moon's life can be summarized in one word: 'suffering itself.' This suffering is not for himself but for God and humanity. Here, we come to know who he is. Rev. Moon is the Messiah, the Savior, and the True Parent of humanity, whom Christianity has hoped for over 2,000 years. Already, disciples in 185 countries around the world are following Rev. Moon with such a confession of faith, striving to walk the path of true children and realize the ideal of true families.
Rev. Moon's identity is verified through his words and life. He possesses a truth that does not exist in the world. The issues of God and humanity, history and the world, and the spirit world are clarified in his words. The promise of new words prophesied in the Bible is fulfilled in him, setting us free. These words contain 'vitality.' Moreover, the more important thing is that Rev. Moon's words are merely an 'interpretation of his own life.' In other words, he himself is the truth. The Word became flesh, that is, incarnated. Therefore, life itself is truth and approaches us through the framework of 'words.'
I am confident that readers will understand the greatness of Rev. Moon through his words. Although the realm of Rev. Moon's words is too high and deep to fully comprehend, it fundamentally has three characteristics.
First, Rev. Moon revealed God through his words and life. He liberated God from silence and suffering. Because humans have an evil lineage, they are God's children but cannot be called children, causing God's pain. Rev. Moon made the sad God, who was tragically alienated due to human sin, 'speak.' He made God, who was silent and trapped in ecclesiastical authority, doctrine, and ornately decorated buildings, 'speak,' and made God, who could not come as the parent of humanity, 'become a parent,' thus Rev. Moon is 'God's complete revelation body.'
Secondly, Rev. Moon liberated humanity from ignorance and chaos. Humans have the ability to think and make value judgments, but they cannot fully explain their own existence, which is a tragic reality. Furthermore, although humans are not independent beings and are interdependent with others, they have not explained this relationality. This is because they lost God's words. Regarding this, Rev. Moon provides the ultimate answer. Moreover, through a life that adheres to the Heavenly Way, he shows a concrete model path. Therefore, his words are living words full of life.
Thirdly, Rev. Moon liberated the world of all things. Every object created by God is an individual truth body with inherent value. Although its value should be fully expressed under the original dominion of the original human, it has not been, causing all things to groan. Through his words, Rev. Moon clarified the original value of the world of all things and opened the way for the liberation of all things by restoring humans to their original state.
Rev. and Mrs. Moon, who came as the eternal True Parents of humanity, continue to give speeches worldwide, demonstrating the teachings of 'use the body of a servant with the heart of a parent' and 'live for the sake of others' through their substantial lives, and work hard to inherit true love, true life, and true lineage.
Furthermore, through the words of life, noble life, and achievements, Rev. Moon finally restored and offered God's kingship with the advent of the new millennium and settled as the King of Blessed Families on this earth. He has been acclaimed as the King of Peace by peace activists from various fields centered on politics and religion worldwide. He also established the Abel UN, the Universal Peace Federation, to realize a new world peace by breaking down the barriers of nations, races, and religions, and is working hard to realize the ideal of a borderless human family of peace in 185 countries worldwide.
I hope that the readers who encounter these words will establish a true value system of life that humanity must pursue, form a true family, and become key players in realizing a true peaceful world in the new millennium as owners of Cheon Il Guk. *
